The House of Chthon
As the corpse of the monstrous entity
Chthon sinks back into the lava whence
it rose, you grip the Rune of Earth
Magic tightly. Now that you have
conquered the Dimension of the Doomed,
realm of Earth Magic, you are ready to
complete your task. A Rune of magic
power lies at the end of each haunted
land of Quake. Go forth, seek the
totality of the four Runes!
As the corpse of the monstrous entity
Chthon sinks back into the lava whence
it rose, you grip the Rune of Earth
Magic tightly. Now that you have
conquered the Dimension of the Doomed,
realm of Earth Magic, you are ready to
complete your task in the other three
haunted lands of Quake. Or are you? If
you don't register Quake, you'll never
know what awaits you in the Realm of
Black Magic, the Netherworld, and the
Elder World!
maps/e2m6.bsp
the Dismal Oubliette
The Rune of Black Magic throbs evilly in
your hand and whispers dark thoughts
into your brain. You learn the inmost
lore of the Hell-Mother; Shub-Niggurath!
You now know that she is behind all the
terrible plotting which has led to so
much death and horror. But she is not
inviolate! Armed with this Rune, you
realize that once all four Runes are
combined, the gate to Shub-Niggurath's
Pit will open, and you can face the
Witch-Goddess herself in her frightful
otherworld cathedral.
maps/e3m6.bsp
Chambers of Torment
The charred viscera of diabolic horrors
bubble viscously as you seize the Rune
of Hell Magic. Its heat scorches your
hand, and its terrible secrets blight
your mind. Gathering the shreds of your
courage, you shake the devil's shackles
from your soul, and become ever more
hard and determined to destroy the
hideous creatures whose mere existence
threatens the souls and psyches of all
the population of Earth.
maps/e4m7.bsp
Azure Agony
Despite the awful might of the Elder
World, you have achieved the Rune of
Elder Magic, capstone of all types of
arcane wisdom. Beyond good and evil,
beyond life and death, the Rune
pulsates, heavy with import. Patient and
potent, the Elder Being Shub-Niggurath
weaves her dire plans to clear off all
life from the Earth, and bring her own
foul offspring to our world! For all the
dwellers in these nightmare dimensions
are her descendants! Once all Runes of
magic power are united, the energy
behind them will blast open the Gateway
to Shub-Niggurath, and you can travel
there to foil the Hell-Mother's plots
in person.
maps/start.bsp
Indian Summer
As you step into the shadows,
a voice echos in your mind...

"Baneslayer, thy return is most welcome
for we are in dire need of thy aid once
more. A great evil has swept across our
land and laid upon it a terrible curse,
which has brought ruin and devastation
to us all. You must destroy the evil
and break the curse, or we will all
perish! Be warned that even thee, our
great champion, are not immune to its
fury, for the enemy knows of thee and
will stop at nothing to destroy thee!
We spirits of the land will shield thee
as best we can, but we cannot stop its
malignant power completely. Go now,
and good luck!"
maps/arcanum5.bsp
You have defeated the master magicians
and banished the eldritch abomination
back whence it came. Unfortunately,
you know it is not dead, and "that
which is not dead can eternal lie."
You realize it is only a matter of
time before another crazy cult tries
to summon the abomination or its kin
back to destroy the Earth. Will you
be able to foil such a plot again,
time after time? Can you?

Even if you can, who will take your
place when you pass away? It feels
you are only delaying the inevitable,
which is the utter annihilation of
Earth by the Great Old Ones. The best
you can hope for is to live a full
life before that dreadful day.
maps/nsoe1.bsp
As you dive into the portal, a deathly
cold chill overwhelms you. You are
frozen in space. With horror, you
watch your combat gear corrode and
disintegrate right before your eyes.
Only your axe, shotgun, and a
handful of shells escape destruction.

As the chill fades, you feel warmth
flood through your body. You can
move again. In fact, you feel like a
new man. Your cuts and bruises have
vanished, as if nothing had happened.
Then, you hear the voice of Mazarbul...

"This is the work of thy enemy! We have
saved thine health and what few weapons
we could. Now, the enemy wages war at
ye City of Angels where thee shall go."
While you knew something was wrong when
you met several of Bane's soldiers back
in the Chamber of Mazarbul, you did
not expect an army of them garrisoned
at the great City of Angels, backed by
emissaries from the former Shal-Rath
Cult, a cult once so powerful they
would have sown chaos and destruction
everywhere had you not slain its
Cult Lord years ago. How could the
land you liberated fall back into
darkness and despair so soon?

Although you and the rebels have won
back the City of Angels, you know your
victory here will be for naught until
you destroy the source of this evil.
Ready to leave, you step into the
pentagram to continue your quest.
maps/nsoe3.bsp
The armies of darkness roam the land
once more -- goblins, Bane's wizards
and warriors, demons from beyond, and
even dragons from the sea and sky.
This can mean only one thing: the
Shal-Rath Cult has returned, and you
wonder in disbelief as to who would be
powerful enough to resurrect so quickly
that which you destroyed years ago.
You know that you must find and destroy
the new Cult Lord before the cult rises
to threaten the multiverse again.
-
And yet, even with their might, they
cannot stop you from liberating The
Lost Land. As you enter the church
tower which they zealously defended,
you discover a strange pool of water.
You dive in to discover the truth...
maps/nsoe4.bsp
So the pool led to a whole subterranean
world! This must be where the Shal-Rath
Cult thrive - the deep, dark underworld.
Obviously this cavern was where they
entered this world - but where was the
Cult Lord? And how did they swarm up
into the world above? The Church Tower
would have been guarded closely by
human armies, if it led to such a
dungeon. There must be another way
up from the underground...

Although you have no idea of the source
of this vile infestation, you have no
doubt that, as is often the case, your
bullets will find their mark. No matter
what, for all these centuries, you
always find the evil you seek and lay
it to permanent, blood-soaked rest...
maps/nsoe5.bsp
In your quest for freedom, you have
fought through hordes of goblins,
armies of Bane's soldiers, packs of
vile beasts, swarms of dragons, and
remnants of the once mighty Shal-Rath
Cult led by a would-be Cult Lord. The
overlord of the forces of darkness
you just vanquished is... Bane?!

Once again you fought the Bane in
mortal combat, and once again you
defeated him and emerged victorious.
Despite your triumph over the Bane
and escape from his domain, you feel
uneasy. How did the Bane return,
and stronger than before?
Then with dread, you wonder
if you will see the Bane again.
Perhaps the Bane has many copies...
The Bane must have used the four Runes
of Quake, those very Runes you used to
slay Shub-Niggurath so long ago, to
resurrect the Shal-Rath Cult, return
them to this ravaged land, and resume
their insidious plan of conquest.
Even though the Bane is gone, he left
the sacred Runes in this stronghold,
guarded by the most fanatical of his
followers and his fiercest dragons.
After an epic battle, even they cannot
stop you, the Baneslayer, from victory.

Now, with the four Runes, you release
their power to banish all of the Bane's
evil and influence from the land. With
the land free, your work here is done.
You step into the teleporter for
a ride with destiny.
maps/roman3.bsp
With the death of Hell's mightiest
warrior, the demonic invasion has
ended. The Earth is safe... for now.

Thus ends this episode of the
slipgate traveler.

You came, you saw, you conquered!

Thank you for playing
A Roman Wilderness of Pain.
You have defeated the dark lord and
ended his terrible reign. Yet, you
feel this is only one of many such
warlords, and another will take his
place someday. Where does Quake find
all of these powerful evil beings?

Over the years, you have confronted
and slain many forms of evil, beginning
with Shub-Niggurath, then moving on to
other eldritch abominations, various
cybernetic demon lords, demented
archmagi, the Bane (twice), and now
this dark lord. Somehow, during the
battle, you felt a connection with him,
as if he was once human. If so, what
caused him to turn away from humanity?
Now, you have all four Runes. You sense
tremendous invisible forces moving to
unseal ancient barriers. Shub-Niggurath
had hoped to use the Runes Herself to
clear off the Earth, but now instead,
you will use them to enter her home and
confront her as an avatar of avenging
Earth-life. If you defeat her, you will
be remembered forever as the savior of
the planet. If she conquers, it will be
as if you had never been born.
--- Soul Of Evil: Indian Summer ---

Dustin `Tronyn` Geeraert

Patrick Martin

As you step through the portal to
leave, visions flash before your eyes!
You see a ranger, much like yourself,
battling four elemental barons. Each
baron wielded mighty power and held a
sacred rune of Quake. One by one, each
baron fell and yielded their rune.
Once the ranger grasped all four runes,
dark forces surged through him. Twisted
by evil, he transcended humanity and
became a dark lord. With newfound
might, he lead the armies of Quake to
conquer many worlds. The visions fade.

You held all four runes before, yet you
did not suffer the evil fate of your
predecessor. For reasons unknown, you
can resist and defeat Quake's power.
Will fortune smile on you next time?

Add_Book
The Log of Lord Ekard

(Press / to turn page.)
Day 50: The Sha'Vile summoned by our
Shal-Rath allies has been a real pain
in the ass! Every week, I lose one or
more of my men to that vile fiend.
However, it is a great executioner,
and the terror it creates helps keep
the locals and some of the more seedy
soldiers among our ranks in line.
Day 67: I had the dubious pleasure of
assigning Acnirt for guard duty in the
dungeon. That shifty slacker always
had a weakness for gambling.
I don't care what the wager was or who
else was involved, but I need men in
that hellhole and Acnirt is as good as
any. It will do him good, if he lives.
Day 68: This wretched rebellion began
ever since the people began shouting
the name of their legendary hero whom
they call the 'Baneslayer'.
For the past few days, the rebel scum
have attacked our army. All prisoners
we take and send to the dungeon for
execution speak of Baneslayer's return.
Day 69: We must find and destroy this
'Baneslayer' before the rebellion gets
out of control. Perhaps we should send
for the dragon to burn the city.

Add_Reflector

Add_Ent
Add_DmStart
item_potion_soe
These chambers were built by the once
great mage Mazarbul. Legend has it
his ghost still haunts his chambers,
punishing the unworthy and the wicked.

Day 67: I lost a bet today and must
pay up 30 qubits and spend a week of
guard duty with that black... thing in
the dungeon. I heard all of the...
horror stories. The beast from Hell,
called the Sha'Vile, loves to mutilate
anyone it can get its vile claws on.

Day 68: The baron brought in several
rebel prisoners. What the beast did to
them was too gruesome to behold -
It played catch with the prisoners...
by casting balls of hellfire at them!
Two of our guards got in the way and
were burnt beyond recognition. Their
horrid screams only amused the beast.
Day 69: That black devil ate one of
our guards and mutilated two more!
I'll be damned if I stay here for
guard duty another day!
Earth Force Heavy Weapons Manual
The MIRV Launcher

(Press / to turn page.)
This big gun launches MIRVs that carry
a payload of five homing rockets.

A MIRV requires 5 rockets to assemble.
Step 1: Press and hold trigger.

This launches the MIRV.
Step 2: Point launcher at targets.

This guides the MIRV where to go. It
also selects targets for the payload.
Step 3: Release trigger.

This releases payload warheads,
which will seek their assigned targets.
Guaranteed results, courtesy of Earth
Force government at taxpayers' expense.
